INIT
{
//  -------  no typ     tip      x    y   z   	 mot  向 状  000+++++++010+++++++020+++++++030+++++++040+++++++050+++++++060+++++++070+++++++080+++++++090+++++++100+++++++110+++++++120+++++++130+++++++140+++++++150+++++++160+++++++170+++++++180+++++++190+++++++200+++++++210+++++++220+++++++230+++++++240+++++++250++
//■A段・扉
//	set_chr( 90,990,	-1,-1,   -15,2307,-450, 180, 2001,	6,"K1_10008;")	//エントリ ワ`ルドマップ
	set_chr( 90,990,	-1,-1,   -15,2307,-450, 180, 2001,	6,"K3_10000;")	//エントリ ワ`ルドマップ
	set_chr( 91,990,	-1,-1,   -9,-2409,200,  0,0201,	6,"K0_11010;")		//エントリ 入口分岐

	//★拉古那はg独行婴蚴激幛俊★社へ向かった米娅を追うことにしたまでは、ダンジョンに入れない。
	if( F4_00_StartSolo && !F4_09_GoShrineMia )
	{
		set_chr( 92,991,	-1,-1,    0,-2200,200,  0,0403,	6,"<EV_STOP_01>")	//ダンジョンに入れないストッパ`
	}
	//第五章中は、艾雯不在之ためダンジョンに入れない
	if( (F4_11_EndFourth && !F5_17_EndFifth)
	{
		set_chr( 92,991,	-1,-1,    0,-2200,200,  0,0403,	6,"<EV_STOP_01>")	//ダンジョンに入れないストッパ`
	}

//■イベント
//	set_chr( 80,990,	-1,-1,   -507,-574,200,  0,0101,	2,"<EV_TEST>")
//	set_chr( 81,990,	-1,-1,    504,-590,200,  0,0101,	2,"<EV_JUMP>")		//イベントジャンプ

//	set_chr( ANNA,40,	-1,-1,   0,-574,200,  	0,0,	20,"<TK_ANNA>")
//	set_chr( ANNA,40,	-1,-1,   0, 243,  0,  	0,0,	20,"<TK_ANNA>")
//	EV("MOVE_ANNA")


/*
	//自颖οI理（トレジャ`）
	#TREASURE_CH	10//トレジャ`用BOX之キャラNO
	#Fx_TREASURE	2301//トレジャ`用フラグ+ル`トNO
	if( Fx_TREASURE )
		set_chr( TREASURE_CH,561,	-1,-1,   0, 243,0,  	 7,270,	0,";")
	else
		set_chr( TREASURE_CH,561,	-1,-1,   0, 243,0,  	 2,270,	20,"<TK_TREASURE>;")

	//自颖οI理（トレジャ`）
	#TAKARA_CH		11//アイテム用BOX之キャラNO
	#IT_TAKARA		30//アイテムNO
	if( IT_TAKARA )
		set_chr( TAKARA_CH,560,	-1,-1,   400, 243,0,  	 6,270,	20,"<TK_TAKARA>;")
	else
		set_chr( TAKARA_CH,560,	-1,-1,   400, 243,0,  	 7,270,	0,";")
*/

	//NPC
	//⑦技を教えてもらっているとき之み嘉兰多が居る
	if(FE_FF_GetSkil_1 && F4_00_StartSolo && !F4_09_GoShrineMia )
	{
		set_chr( GYARANDOW,21,	-1,-1,  -9,-279,101,	51,0,		20,"<TK_GYARANDOW>")	//嘉兰多
		F_set_chr(GYARANDOW,CF_NO_MOVE)
	}
	

	//③３妖精
	if( F2_00_GoForest && !F2_14_TalkEnemy)
	{
//		set_chr( SPIRIT_A,84,	-1,-1,	-465,157,0,		 15,314, 20,"<TK_SPIRIT_A>")	//玛琳
//		set_chr( SPIRIT_B,85,	-1,-1,	-261,131,1,	 15,33, 20,"<TK_SPIRIT_B>")	//莉琪
//		set_chr( SPIRIT_C,86,	-1,-1,	-296,378,0,	 15,151, 20,"<TK_SPIRIT_C>")	//修
		set_chr( SPIRIT_A,84,	-1,-1,	-266,-261,100,		 15,175, 20,"<TK_SPIRIT_A>")	//玛琳
		set_chr( SPIRIT_B,85,	-1,-1,	-143,215,0,			 15,161, 20,"<TK_SPIRIT_B>")	//莉琪
		set_chr( SPIRIT_C,86,	-1,-1,	-296,378,0,			 15,205, 20,"<TK_SPIRIT_C>")	//修
		F_set_chr(SPIRIT_A,CF_NO_MOVE)
		F_set_chr(SPIRIT_B,CF_NO_MOVE)
		F_set_chr(SPIRIT_C,CF_NO_MOVE)
	}

	if(GW_ENTRY_EVENT==1)
	{
		workG(GW_ENTRY_EVENT,SET,0)
		//坑を出て罗亚鲁塔村へ
		set_namebmp(0,0)
		EV("EV_1_06_GoVillage")
	}
	else
	if(F1_02_EndPrologue && !F1_22_EndFirst)
	{
	//１章

		{
			//塞肯多姆废坑に到着する
			EV("EV_1_00_OnCave")
		}
	}

//■场面固有O定
}

MOVE_ANNA
{
	move( ANNA, 25,	6,	1000,1000,0,	200)
	wait_move( ANNA )
	wait(50)
	loop
}

EV_V3_TEST
{
	EV_begin()

	CAM_move(110,899,229,0,0)
	CAM(-130,54,229,20,279,0,0)

	chr_pos(RAGNA,217,-1025,100,39,2)
	KAO(PARTNER,"1","1","1")//デフォルト

	chr_pos(PARTNER,-9,-759,100,223,2)
//	chr_pos(PARTNER,-9,-759,100,39,2)
	KAO(PARTNER,"1","1","1")//デフォルト

	wait(30)

	MOT(PARTNER,50,15)

	SE(500,PARTNER)
	KAO(PARTNER,"14641Z7","1236","1")//デフォルト
	MES_pos(PARTNER,"S6C1艾雯「真是不错的舞蹈呢」",1,	300,420,0,0)
	wait(70)
	MES_close(PARTNER)

	MOT(RAGNA,53,15)

	SE(501,RAGNA)
	MES_pos(RAGNA,"S6C1拉古那「呀～　来了吗」",1,	320,420,0,0)
	wait(70)
	MES_close(RAGNA)

	MOT(PARTNER,2,15)

	SE(502,PARTNER)
	KAO(PARTNER,"14641ZH","62112321","1")//デフォルト
	MES_pos(PARTNER,"S6C1艾雯「因为、就算在村里也不会退缩」",1,	300,420,0,0)
	wait(90)
	MES_close(PARTNER)

	SE(503,RAGNA)
	MES_pos(RAGNA,"S6C1拉古那「你好象变了呢」",1,	300,420,0,0)
	wait(60)
	MES_close(RAGNA)

	SE(504,PARTNER)
	KAO(PARTNER,"14641Z3","12","12")//デフォルト
	MES_pos(PARTNER,"S6C1艾雯「什么啊 ？」",1,	300,420,0,0)
	wait(40)
	MES_close(PARTNER)

	SE(505,RAGNA)
	MES_pos(PARTNER,"S6C1拉古那「因为老是说很怕鬼的」",1,	300,420,0,0)
	wait(90)
	MES_close(RAGNA)

	SE(506,PARTNER)
	KAO(PARTNER,"14641Z7","3N","21")//デフォルト
	MES_pos(PARTNER,"S6C1艾雯「那脸才不吓人哪」",1,	300,420,0,0)
	wait(60)
	MES_close(PARTNER)

	//モ`ションセット(登h)
	MOT_SET(RAGNA,150,151,990,1024,-1,-1)
	MOT_SET(RAGNA,151,-2,1024,1024,-1,-1)
	MOT(RAGNA,150,15)

	CAM(-130,64,229,20,279,10,0)
	CAM_quake("464646")

	SE(507,RAGNA)
	KAO(RAGNA,"5","5","5")//ガ`ン
//	MES_pos(RAGNA,"P1S7が`ん！！真过分",0,	500,150,0,0)
	MES_pos(RAGNA,"S6C1拉古那「咔！！吓人吧」",1,	300,420,0,0)
	wait(60)
	MES_close(RAGNA)
	stop_SE(507,RAGNA)

//	wait(60)

//	loop

	CAM_return( 30 )
	wait( 30 )


	EV_end()

}

}

//──────────────────────────────
//塞肯多姆废坑に到着する
//──────────────────────────────
//　　坑入口に入ったところでイベント_始。
//　　地名表示を出しながらh景でマップ之荬蛞せつつ、
//　　拉古那と艾雯が入ってくる之をせる。
EV_1_00_OnCave
{
	EV_begin()

	//暗
	fade_in(100,1,0)
	wait_fade()

	//キャラ再配置
	chr_pos(RAGNA,136,804,-9,180,2)
	chr_pos(PARTNER,0,670,-3,180,2)
	color(RAGNA,-1)
	color(PARTNER,-1)

	set_chr(EVENT_RAGNA,	  1010,-1,-1, 110,400,0, 2,180,0, "")
	set_chr(ALWEN, 	 	1011,-1,-1, -60,370,0, 2, 180,0, "")
	F_set_chr(EVENT_RAGNA,CF_NO_CLIP)
	F_set_chr(EVENT_RAGNA,CF_NO_CLIP2)
	F_set_chr(EVENT_RAGNA,CF_NO_CSP)
	F_set_chr(ALWEN,CF_NO_CLIP)
	F_set_chr(ALWEN,CF_NO_CLIP2)
	F_set_chr(ALWEN,CF_NO_CSP)
	color(EVENT_RAGNA,-1)
	color(ALWEN,-1)

	KAO(EVENT_RAGNA,"1","1","1")//デフォルト
	KAO(ALWEN,"1","1","1")//デフォルト

	//モ`ション定x
	MOT_SET(ALWEN,150,-1,399,399,-1,-1)//腰に手を当てる（左）

	wait(1)
	chr_equip( ALWEN,"wp_004", "Bone_RightSword", 100)	//杖を装浃丹护胫はこちら。
//	MOT(ALWEN,53,1)										//艾雯之右手を_かせる

	//カメラ初期位置
	CAM_move(-36,-1182,83,0,0)
	CAM(590,89,30,36,180,0,0)

	fade_in(0,60,0)	//フェ`ドイン
	CAM_move(31,1024,600,	300,2)
	CAM(-450,105,330,35,200,300,1)
	wait_CAM_move()

	cross_fade(30)
	CAM_move(-86,800,380,0,0)
	CAM(-250,108,380,28,152,0,0)
	CAM(-250,80,380,28,152,500,0)

	color(EVENT_RAGNA,1)
	color(ALWEN,1)
	move( EVENT_RAGNA, 0,	9, 110,-696,100,0)
	wait(30)
	move( ALWEN, 0,	9,-100,-666,100,0)
	wait_move( EVENT_RAGNA)
	wait( 30 )

	MES(EVENT_RAGNA,"这里是……",0)
	MES_close(EVENT_RAGNA)
	wait_MES(EVENT_RAGNA)

	cross_fade(15)
	CAM_move(-40,760,240,0,0)
	CAM(-50,58,240,22,38,0,0)
	CAM_move(-40,720,240,900,0)
	CAM(-170,58,240,22,52,900,0)
	wait(15)

	MOT(ALWEN,150,15)
	wait(15)
	KAO(ALWEN,"12321Z8","1233321","1")//
	MES(ALWEN,"《塞肯多姆废坑》……\n古代的时候、地之妖精诺姆所建造的\n魔宝石坑道遗迹。",0)
	KAO(ALWEN,"12321Z8","1","1")//
	MES(ALWEN,"在矿脉开采尽后、\n诺姆他们就移住\n到其他地方了……",0)
	MES_close(ALWEN)

	MOT(EVENT_RAGNA,53,15)
	wait(15)
	KAO(EVENT_RAGNA,"12321Z3","12332A","6")//
	MES(EVENT_RAGNA,"哦、诺姆吗……",0)
	KAO(EVENT_RAGNA,"12321Z5","A","6")//
	MES(EVENT_RAGNA,"虽然听起来很有意思\n但是我不认为它存在。",0)
	MES_close(EVENT_RAGNA)

	MOT(EVENT_RAGNA,2,15)
	rot(EVENT_RAGNA, 30,150)
	look_chr( EVENT_RAGNA, ALWEN ,"Bone_Head")
	wait(15)
	KAO(EVENT_RAGNA,"12321Z5","23332","1")//
	MES(EVENT_RAGNA,"不过、虽然那么说\n但是还有吸血鬼存在的话。",0)
	MES_close(EVENT_RAGNA)

	MOT(ALWEN,2,15)//デフォルト
	wait(15)
	KAO(ALWEN,"E","123332","3")//
	MES(ALWEN,"…………………………………",0)
	MES_close(ALWEN)

//　　拉古那之^に？マ`ク。
	KAO(EVENT_RAGNA,"E","1","9")//
	EMO(EVENT_RAGNA,EMO_HATENA)
	wait(15)
	rot(EVENT_RAGNA, 30,120)
	wait(15)
	KAO(EVENT_RAGNA,"12321Z3","1233321","1")//
	MES(EVENT_RAGNA,"怎么了、发生什么事了？",0)
	MES_close(EVENT_RAGNA)

	look_chr( ALWEN, EVENT_RAGNA ,"Bone_Head")
	wait(15)
	KAO(ALWEN,"B232BZ5","233333321","2")//
	MES(ALWEN,"……虽然很微弱\n但是感觉到我的魔力了。",0)
	MES_close(ALWEN)
	wait_MES(ALWEN)
	
	cross_fade(15)
	CAM_move(6,1420,400,0,0)
	CAM(-490,98,400,30,180,0,0)
	CAM_move(6,1420,400,600,0)
	CAM(-490,110,400,28,180,600,0)
	look_off(ALWEN)
	wait_fade()

	MES(ALWEN,"从这里面出来的。",0)
	MES_close(ALWEN)

//　　拉古那之^に！マ`ク。
	KAO(EVENT_RAGNA,"D","D","3")//
	EMO(EVENT_RAGNA,EMO_BIKKURI)
	wait(15)
	rot(EVENT_RAGNA, 30,180)
	look_off(EVENT_RAGNA)
	wait(15)
	MES(EVENT_RAGNA,"真的吗！？",0)
	MES_close(EVENT_RAGNA)

	MES(ALWEN,"嗯、在城附近感觉到的气息\n就应该是这里了。",0)
	MES(ALWEN,"似乎、只有被夺取魔力的\n一部分在这里……",0)
	MES_close(ALWEN)

	MOT(EVENT_RAGNA,50,15)
	wait(15)
	MES(EVENT_RAGNA,"不是太明白\n不过应该有值钱的东西吧？",0)
	MES(EVENT_RAGNA,"所以不要多说了。\n先去里面调查吧。",0)
	MES_close(EVENT_RAGNA)

	MES(ALWEN,"うむ。",0)
	MES_close(ALWEN)

//　　イベントK了、プレイヤ`操作S可。
	fade_in( 100, 30, BLACK)	//暗
	wait_fade()

	delete(EVENT_RAGNA)
	delete(ALWEN)

	chr_pos(RAGNA,110,-696,100,180,2)
	chr_pos(PARTNER,-100,-666,100,180,2)
	color(RAGNA,1)
	color(PARTNER,1)

	CAM_return( 0 )
	wait( 30 )

//ＧＦ『★塞肯多姆废坑に到着した』を立てる。
	F_set(F1_10_OnCave)

	fade_in( 0, 30, BLACK)	//フェ`ドイン

	EV_end()

}
//──────────────────────────────
//坑を出て罗亚鲁塔村へ
//──────────────────────────────
//　　暗してしばらくしてから、
//　　画面フェ`ドインして、坑入口マップ。
//　　坑内部から出てきた拉古那、艾雯、露を映す。
EV_1_06_GoVillage
{
	EV_begin()

	//暗
	fade_in(100,1,0)
	wait_fade()

	//キャラ再配置
	chr_pos(RAGNA,-138,-1054,100,330,2)
	chr_pos(PARTNER,40,-1014,100,0,2)
	color(RAGNA,-1)
	color(PARTNER,-1)

	set_chr(EVENT_RAGNA,	  1010,-1,-1, -138,-1054,100, 2,330,0, "")
	set_chr(ALWEN, 	 	1011,-1,-1, 40,-1014,100, 2, 0,0, "")
	F_set_chr(EVENT_RAGNA,CF_NO_CLIP)
	F_set_chr(EVENT_RAGNA,CF_NO_CLIP2)
	F_set_chr(EVENT_RAGNA,CF_NO_CSP)
	F_set_chr(ALWEN,CF_NO_CLIP)
	F_set_chr(ALWEN,CF_NO_CLIP2)
	F_set_chr(ALWEN,CF_NO_CSP)

	//イベント用キャラ配置
	set_chr( LUE,		 1015,-1,-1, 20,-744,100, 2,	180,	0,"")	//露
	F_set_chr(LUE,CF_NO_CLIP)
	F_set_chr(LUE,CF_NO_CLIP2)
	F_set_chr(LUE,CF_NO_CSP)
	F_set_chr(LUE,CF_NO_HEIGHT)

				wait_MES(RAGNA)
			}
			F_set(F5_24_NotDanjion)
		}
		else
		{
		//　　※２回目以降は以下之メッセ`ジ。
			MES(RAGNA,"进入地城找的话\n应该很费劲……",0)
			MES(RAGNA,"首先先找找看\n应该会有的地方好了。",0)
			MES_close(RAGNA)
			wait_MES(RAGNA)
		}
		chr_pos(PET,-156,-1941,200,0,2)
	}
	else
	if( !F5_17_EndFifth )
	{
//	name("・水晶峡谷起俞")

		if( GW_MAN==1 )
		{
		//　　※拉古那先^
			if( !F_RAGNA )
			{
				rot_chr(PET,30,RAGNA)
				MES(PET,"拉古那、想去那里啊！",0)
				MES(PET,"快点去帮助公主啊！",0)
				MES_close(PET)

				rot_chr(RAGNA,30,PET)
			//	name2(RAGNA)
				MES(RAGNA,"啊啊、是呢。",0)
				MES(RAGNA,"不早点准备好、\n去水晶峡谷的话。",0)
				MES_close(RAGNA)
				wait_MES(RAGNA)
				F_set(RAGNA)
			}
			else
			{
			//　　★Rり返し
				MES(RAGNA,"不早点准备好、\n去救公主可不行！",0)
				MES_close(RAGNA)
				wait_MES(RAGNA)
			}
		}
		else
		{
		//　　※奥蒂莎先^
			if( !F_RAGNA )
			{
				rot_chr(PET,30,PARTNER)
				MES(PET,"等一下狼女、你想去那里啊！",0)
				MES(PET,"快点去帮公主！",0)
				MES_close(PET)

				rot_chr(PARTNER,30,PET)
			//	name2(PARTNER)
				MES(PARTNER,"哈哈、知道了。",0)
				MES(PARTNER,"马上准备好、\n就去大家那里。",0)
				MES_close(PARTNER)
				wait_MES(PARTNER)
				F_set(RAGNA)
			}
			else
			{
			//　　★Rり返し
				MES(PARTNER,"没时间绕弯子了……",0)
				MES(PARTNER,"不快点准备好、\n不去大家那里可不行。",0)
				MES_close(PARTNER)
				wait_MES(PARTNER)
			}
		}
		//奥蒂莎がいる
		if(F5_08_JoinOdessa && !F5_13_KillDygald)
		{
			chr_pos(PLAYER2,156,-1941,200,,0,2)
		}
		chr_pos(PET,-156,-1941,200,0,2)
	}
	//chr_pos(PLAYER,4,-1779,200,0,2)
	chr_pos(PLAYER1,4,-1779,200,0,2)
	
	gather_party(RAGNA)
	CAM_return(0)
	cross_fade( 30 )
	wait_fade()	

	TK_end()

}
